\"badgeClass\": get_class_name_from_most_common_category_color(element[2]),\n                        \"url\": \"#modal-event-group\"\n                };\n            });\n            $(\".responsive-calendar\").responsiveCalendar({\n                    time: (year+'-'+month),\n                    events: events\n            });\n        }\n\n        function          type: 'GET',\n                url: url,\n                dataType: 'json',\n                data: {\n                    year: year,\n                    month: month\n                },\n                success: function(data) {\n                    set_calendar(month, year, data);\n                },\n                error: function(data) {\n                    set_calendar(month, year, data);\n                }\n            });\n        }\n\n        get_event_count_for_each_day(month, year);\n\n        function get_events_for_clicked_day(day, month, year){\n            var domain = get_class_name_from_most_common_category_color(color) {\n            class_name = 'event-poland';\n            if (color=='blue') {\n                class_name = 'event-business';\n            }\n {\n          var time = 7; // time in seconds\n          var $progressBar,\n            $bar,\n            $elem,\n            isPause,\n            tick,\n            percentTime;\n          $(\"#einsert-owl-cl\").owlCarousel({\n            slideSpeed: 500,\n            paginationSpeed: 500,\n            singleItem: true,\n            navigation: true,\n            afterInit: progressBar,\n            afterMove: moved,\n            startDragging: pauseOnDragging\n          });\n          function progressBar(elem) {\n              $elem = elem;\n              buildProgressBar();\n              start();\n            }\n          function buildProgressBar() {\n            $progressBar = $(\"<div>\", {\n              id: \"progressBar\"\n            });\n            $bar = $(\"<div>\", {\n              id: \"bar\"\n            });\n            $progressBar.append($bar).prependTo($elem);\n          }\n\n          function start() {\n            percentTime = 0;\n            isPause = false;\n            tick = setInterval(interval, 10);\n          };\n\n          function interval() {\n              if (isPause === false) {\n                percentTime += 1 / time;\n                $bar.css({\n                  width: percentTime + \"%\"\n                });\n                if (percentTime >= 100) {\n                  $elem.trigger('owl.next')\n
